Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: 
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: Increased homocysteine can be a risk factor for heart disease. Supplementing with active B vitamins will help to bring your homocysteine down to a more optimal level. Phytomulti is a good multivitamin containing all the necessary B vitamins.

Doctor: Christie Pilossof
Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: 
Women's Health Recommendations: 
Overview Notes: An increased waist circumference is associated with an increased risk of chronic disease such as heart disease and diabetes. Losing weight, specifically around your abdomen will help to negate this risk and lower your fasting insulin too. Watch the starch and sugar in your diet.
Comment Key: MedicalHistoryNote
Comment Value: Anthony with your family history of heart disease and raised cholesterol and numerous other risk factors for heart disease i think it is prudent that you continue your follow ups with the cardiologist and try to lose weight, improve your diet and continue to exercise. We want to get the insulin levels under control and prevent progression to type 2 diabetes. Please repeat your bloods in 3 months and then we can follow up from there. It was a pleasure to do your medical today and we look forward to helping you have a healthier 2022!
Special Investigation Notes: Stress ECG and Lung function test not done, body fat percentage above normal (aim for less than 24%)

Overview Notes: Supplement with vitamin D3 5000 iu daily. Retest level in 3 months. Aim for a level of 50 to 80ug and then reduce supplement to 1000iu daily. Vitamin D is important for your bones, mood, acts as an anti-inflammatory and has been shown to decrease the severity and improve outcomes with covid 19.
Comment Key: SymptomScreeningNote
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Stress ECG and Lung function test not done, body fat percentage above normal (aim for less than 24%)
